
# AssetConversion

---------
## Calls

---------
### add_liquidity
See [`Pallet::add_liquidity`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset1 | `T::MultiAssetId` | 
| asset2 | `T::MultiAssetId` | 
| amount1_desired | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount2_desired | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount1_min | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount2_min | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| mint_to | `T::AccountId` | 

#### Python

---------
### create_pool
See [`Pallet::create_pool`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset1 | `T::MultiAssetId` | 
| asset2 | `T::MultiAssetId` |

---------
### remove_liquidity
See [`Pallet::remove_liquidity`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| asset1 | `T::MultiAssetId` | 
| asset2 | `T::MultiAssetId` | 
| lp_token_burn | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount1_min_receive | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount2_min_receive | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| withdraw_to | `T::AccountId` |

---------
### swap_exact_tokens_for_tokens
See [`Pallet::swap_exact_tokens_for_tokens`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| path | `BoundedVec<T::MultiAssetId, T::MaxSwapPathLength>` | 
| amount_in | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount_out_min | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| send_to | `T::AccountId` | 
| keep_alive | `bool` |

### swap_tokens_for_exact_tokens
See [`Pallet::swap_tokens_for_exact_tokens`].
#### Attributes
| Name | Type |
| -------- | -------- | 
| path | `BoundedVec<T::MultiAssetId, T::MaxSwapPathLength>` | 
| amount_out | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| amount_in_max | `T::AssetBalance` | 
| send_to | `T::AccountId` | 
| keep_alive | `bool` |

---------
## Events

---------
### LiquidityAdded
A successful call of the `AddLiquidity` extrinsic will create this event.
#### Attributes
| Name | Type | Composition
| -------- | -------- | -------- |
| who | `T::AccountId` | ```AccountId```
| mint_to | `T::AccountId` | ```AccountId```

---------
### LiquidityRemoved
A successful call of the `RemoveLiquidity` extrinsic will create this event.
#### Attributes
| Name | Type | Composition
| -------- | -------- | -------- |
| who | `T::AccountId` | ```AccountId```

---------

---------
### SwapExecuted
Assets have been converted from one to another. Both `SwapExactTokenForToken`
and `SwapTokenForExactToken` will generate this event.
#### Attributes
| Name | Type | Composition
| -------- | -------- | -------- |
| who | `T::AccountId` | ```AccountId```
| send_to | `T::AccountId` | ```AccountId```
| path | `BoundedVec<T::MultiAssetId, T::MaxSwapPathLength>` | ```[{'parents': 'u8', 'interior': {'Here': None, 'X1': {'Parachain': 'u32', 'AccountId32': 'InnerStruct', 'AccountIndex64': 'InnerStruct', 'AccountKey20': 'InnerStruct', 'PalletInstance': 'u8', 'GeneralIndex': 'u128', 'GeneralKey': 'InnerStruct', 'OnlyChild': None, 'Plurality': 'InnerStruct', 'GlobalConsensus': 'scale_info::41'}, 'X2': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38'), 'X3': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38'), 'X4': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38'), 'X5': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38'), 'X6': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38'), 'X7': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38'), 'X8': ('scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38', 'scale_info::38')}}]```
| amount_in | `T::AssetBalance` | ```u128```
| amount_out | `T::AssetBalance` | ```u128```

| amount | `T::AssetBalance` | ```u128```

---------
## Storage functions

---------
### NextPoolAssetId
 Stores the `PoolAssetId` that is going to be used for the next lp token.
 This gets incremented whenever a new lp pool is created.

#### Python
```python
result = substrate.query(
    'AssetConversion', 'NextPoolAssetId', []
)
```

#### Return value
```python
'u32'
```
---------
### Pools
 Map from `PoolAssetId` to `PoolInfo`. This establishes whether a pool has been officially
 created rather than people sending tokens directly to a pool&#x27;s public account.

#### Python
```python
result = substrate.query(
    'AssetConversion', 'Pools', [
    (
        {
            'interior': {
                'Here': None,
                'X1': {
                    'AccountId32': {
                        'id': '[u8; 32]',
                        'network': (
                            None,
                            'scale_info::41',
                        ),
                    },
                    'AccountIndex64': {
                        'index': 'u64',
                        'network': (
                            None,
                            'scale_info::41',
                        ),
                    },
                    'AccountKey20': {
                        'key': '[u8; 20]',
                        'network': (
                            None,
                            'scale_info::41',
                        ),
                    },
                    'GeneralIndex': 'u128',
                    'GeneralKey': {
                        'data': '[u8; 32]',
                        'length': 'u8',
                    },
                    'GlobalConsensus': {
                        'BitcoinCash': None,
                        'BitcoinCore': None,
                        'ByFork': {
                            'block_hash': '[u8; 32]',
                            'block_number': 'u64',
                        },
                        'ByGenesis': '[u8; 32]',
                        'Ethereum': {
                            'chain_id': 'u64',
                        },
                        'Kusama': None,
                        'Polkadot': None,
                        'Rococo': None,
                        'Westend': None,
                        'Wococo': None,
                    },
                    'OnlyChild': None,
                    'PalletInstance': 'u8',
                    'Parachain': 'u32',
                    'Plurality': {
                        'id': {
                            'Administration': None,
                            'Defense': None,
                            'Executive': None,
                            'Index': 'u32',
                            'Judicial': None,
                            'Legislative': None,
                            'Moniker': '[u8; 4]',
                            'Technical': None,
                            'Treasury': None,
                            'Unit': None,
                        },
                        'part': {
                            'AtLeastProportion': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Fraction': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Members': 'InnerStruct',
                            'MoreThanProportion': 'InnerStruct',
                            'Voice': None,
                        },
                    },
                },
                'X2': (
```

#### Return value
```python
{'lp_token': 'u32'}
```

---------
## Constants

---------
### AllowMultiAssetPools
 A setting to allow creating pools with both non-native assets.
#### Value
```python
False
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'AllowMultiAssetPools')
```
---------
### LPFee
 A % the liquidity providers will take of every swap. Represents 10ths of a percent.
#### Value
```python
3
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'LPFee')
```
---------
### LiquidityWithdrawalFee
 A fee to withdraw the liquidity.
#### Value
```python
0
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'LiquidityWithdrawalFee')
```
---------
### MaxSwapPathLength
 The max number of hops in a swap.
#### Value
```python
4
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'MaxSwapPathLength')
```
---------
### MintMinLiquidity
 The minimum LP token amount that could be minted. Ameliorates rounding errors.
#### Value
```python
100
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'MintMinLiquidity')
```
---------
### PalletId
 The pallet&#x27;s id, used for deriving its sovereign account ID.
#### Value
```python
'0x70792f6173636f6e'
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'PalletId')
```
---------
### PoolSetupFee
 A one-time fee to setup the pool.
#### Value
```python
0
```
#### Python
```python
constant = substrate.get_constant('AssetConversion', 'PoolSetupFee')
```
---------
## Errors

---------
### AmountOneLessThanMinimal
Provided amount should be greater than or equal to the existential deposit/asset&\#x27;s
minimal amount.

---------
### AmountOutTooHigh
Desired amount can&\#x27;t be equal to the pool reserve.

---------
### AmountTwoLessThanMinimal
Provided amount should be greater than or equal to the existential deposit/asset&\#x27;s
minimal amount.

---------
### AssetOneDepositDidNotMeetMinimum
The minimal amount requirement for the first token in the pair wasn&\#x27;t met.

---------
### AssetOneWithdrawalDidNotMeetMinimum
The minimal amount requirement for the first token in the pair wasn&\#x27;t met.

---------
### AssetTwoDepositDidNotMeetMinimum
The minimal amount requirement for the second token in the pair wasn&\#x27;t met.

---------
### AssetTwoWithdrawalDidNotMeetMinimum
The minimal amount requirement for the second token in the pair wasn&\#x27;t met.

---------
### CorrespondenceError
Unable to find an element in an array/vec that should have one-to-one correspondence
with another. For example, an array of assets constituting a `path` should have a
corresponding array of `amounts` along the path.

---------
### EqualAssets
Provided assets are equal.

---------
### IncorrectPoolAssetId
It was not possible to get or increment the Id of the pool.

---------
### InsufficientLiquidity
Insufficient liquidity in the pool.

---------
### InsufficientLiquidityMinted
Insufficient liquidity minted.

---------
### InvalidPath
The provided path must consists of 2 assets at least.

---------
### NonUniquePath
The provided path must consists of unique assets.

---------
### OptimalAmountLessThanDesired
Optimal calculated amount is less than desired.

---------
### Overflow
An overflow happened.

---------
### PathError
It was not possible to calculate path data.

---------
### PoolExists
Pool already exists.

---------
### PoolMustContainNativeCurrency
Only pools with native on one side are valid.

---------
### PoolNotFound
The pool doesn&\#x27;t exist.

---------
### ProvidedMaximumNotSufficientForSwap
Provided maximum amount is not sufficient for swap.

---------
### ProvidedMinimumNotSufficientForSwap
Calculated amount out is less than provided minimum amount.

---------
### ReserveLeftLessThanMinimal
Reserve needs to always be greater than or equal to the existential deposit/asset&\#x27;s
minimal amount.

---------
### UnsupportedAsset
Provided asset is not supported for pool.

---------
### WrongDesiredAmount
Desired amount can&\#x27;t be zero.

---------
### ZeroAmount
Amount can&\#x27;t be zero.

---------
### ZeroLiquidity
Requested liquidity can&\#x27;t be zero.

---------
